Expanding: **7.317 * epsilon^3 + 7.950 * T * exp(-epsilon) - 2282.4 * exp(-epsilon)**

The GT has three basis functions:
1. **epsilon^3** (polynomial in epsilon only)
2. **T * exp(-epsilon)** (T times exponential)
3. **exp(-epsilon)** (exponential, no T)

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

For each candidate, I need to check if the functional forms (basis functions) can reproduce these three terms exactly.

**Key observations about GT structure:**
- The T-dependence is purely through `T * exp(-epsilon)` — linear in T with exp(-epsilon) coefficient
- There's a pure `epsilon^3` term
- There's a pure `exp(-epsilon)` term

Let me go through candidates:

### Candidate 1: T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*epsilon*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*log(c5*epsilon+1) + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*epsilon+c9))

T-dependent terms: c0*T + c1*T*epsilon. GT needs T*exp(-epsilon). Since T*exp(-epsilon) ≠ a*T + b*T*epsilon for all epsilon, this cannot match.

Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 2: T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + T*c2*log(c3*epsilon+1) + c4*epsilon*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6*exp(c7*epsilon)*sin(c8*epsilon+c9)

T-dependent: c0*T + c1*T*epsilon + c2*T*log(c3*epsilon+1). Cannot reproduce T*exp(-epsilon).

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 3: T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*epsilon*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*epsilon+c7)) + c8*exp(T*c9)

T-dependent: c0*T + c1*T*epsilon + c8*exp(c9*T). Cannot reproduce T*exp(-epsilon).

Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 4: T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*epsilon + c3*exp(c4*sin(c5*epsilon+c6)) + c7*epsilon*exp(c8*epsilon)

T-dependent: c0*T + c1*T*epsilon. Cannot match T*exp(-epsilon).

Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 5: T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*epsilon + c3*log(c4*exp(c5*epsilon)+1) + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*epsilon+c9))

T-dependent: c0*T + c1*T*epsilon. Cannot match.

Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 11: T*c0*exp(c1*epsilon) + T*c2 + c3*log(c4*epsilon+1) + c5*epsilon/(c6+c7*exp(c8*epsilon))

T-dependent: c0*T*exp(c1*epsilon) + c2*T. Setting c1 = -1 gives T*exp(-epsilon) term, and c2*T is constant in epsilon.

So T-part: c0*T*exp(-epsilon) + c2*T. GT T-part: 7.950*T*exp(-epsilon). Set c0=7.950, c2=0.

Non-T part: c3*log(c4*epsilon+1) + c5*epsilon/(c6+c7*exp(c8*epsilon))

GT non-T part: 7.317*epsilon^3 - 2282.4*exp(-epsilon)

Can log and rational-exponential terms produce epsilon^3 - const*exp(-epsilon)? No — log(c4*epsilon+1) is a logarithmic function, not polynomial. Cannot match epsilon^3.

### Candidate 12: T*c0*log(c1*epsilon+1) + T*c2*epsilon + T^c3*c4*sin(c5*epsilon+c6) + c7 + c8/T^5

### Candidate 14: T*c0*sqrt(c1+epsilon^2) + T*c2*sin(c3*epsilon+c4) + T^c5*c6*exp(c7*epsilon) + c8*sqrt(c1+epsilon^2)

Setting c5=1: all terms are T*f(epsilon). Then T*(c0*sqrt(c1+epsilon^2) + c2*sin(c3*epsilon+c4) + c6*exp(c7*epsilon)) needs to equal 7.950*T*exp(-epsilon).

So c0*sqrt(c1+epsilon^2) + c2*sin(c3*epsilon+c4) + c6*exp(c7*epsilon) = 7.950*exp(-epsilon).

Set c0=0, c2=0, c6=7.950, c7=-1. Then T-part works.

Non-T part: c8*sqrt(c1+epsilon^2). With c0=0, c1 is free. Need c8*sqrt(c1+epsilon^2) = 7.317*epsilon^3 - 2282.4*exp(-epsilon). sqrt cannot produce epsilon^3.
